  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2460ab20-a9e8-4891-a9df-246ce2286072'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer17225202782169497822">I thought things were bad and weird before—hold on—it’s getting worse.<br/><br/>Adam and I are both going through identity crises of epic proportions as we Transition from who we were, and discover who we were meant to be.   <span id="freeText17225202782169497822" style="display:none">I thought things were bad and weird before—hold on—it’s getting worse.<br /><br />Adam and I are both going through identity crises of epic proportions as we Transition from who we were, and discover who we were meant to be. More Fae are dying, and I feel as if time is running out for us to find all of those responsible and put an end to the killings.<br /><br />The people I thought I could trust have betrayed me and the one person I should absolutely not trust is taking me deeper and deeper into his world.<br /><br />Ryder’s secrets are dangerous and devastating.<br /><br />With each touch and word, he pulls my heart closer to himself and at the same time he is trying to keep me at arm’s length. The dance he and I have begun, is getting more complicated as our worlds are being shaken from all sides, and the visions of the future are frightening, and nothing like I had ever pictured for myself or those I care for.<br /><br />This time, destiny is taunting me.<br /><br />I had always thought that I controlled my destiny. Now, my rights are being taken from me by powerful people and leaving me with alternatives that range between bad and awful.<br /><br />This time, the choices I have to make can decide the fate of both worlds.<br /><br />Everything is unraveling, and nothing will ever be the same again.</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">You should definitely start from the first book. The second one picks up straight after the first, which would mean that reading this book first would<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">You should definitely start from the first book. The second one picks up straight after the first, which would mean that reading this book first would be extremely confusing. Hope that answers your question. :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12673185333467593068"><b>Re-read: 21.10.14</b><br/><b>Second re-read: 24.04.15</b><br/>Ohh sweet baby jesus! I'm losing it here!!!! Amelia, how can you let it end like this?! Where was he, what's going on, what will happen?! All these questions in my head, and I'm freaking out!!!! I need to know, like NOW! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304066ra/17120206.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Is everything lost? Will Ryder save her? What will the Horde King do? Why didn't he come? What will my Prince of Dark Fae do? Syn and Ryder.. Ryder and Syn.. Ryder… I need more! I miss them already!!!!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304095ra/17120210.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Ryder never disappoints, sexy, domina</span>
  <span id="freeText12673185333467593068" style="display:none"><b>Re-read: 21.10.14</b><br><b>Second re-read: 24.04.15</b><br>Ohh sweet baby jesus! I'm losing it here!!!! Amelia, how can you let it end like this?! Where was he, what's going on, what will happen?! All these questions in my head, and I'm freaking out!!!! I need to know, like NOW! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304066ra/17120206.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Is everything lost? Will Ryder save her? What will the Horde King do? Why didn't he come? What will my Prince of Dark Fae do? Syn and Ryder.. Ryder and Syn.. Ryder… I need more! I miss them already!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304095ra/17120210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ryder never disappoints, sexy, dominant, dangerous, snarky, sex god, yet still so.. loving! I want him. He's probably everything I want, and everything my parents would hate.. :P Ryder's still a fucking mystery, and I'm loving it while being frustrated at the same time.. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304356ra/17120230.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He's MINE btw. I just wanted to mention that.. So stay the hell away from him.. Except Syn, my sweet Syn, so awesome, kick ass heroine, bloody brilliant warrior with her fantastic mouth! I love everything that comes out of her mouth, all of her comments are just so freaking perfect! She's so independent and strong. Everyone, everything is trying to bring her down, but she always get up, and becomes a stronger woman. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304810ra/17120276.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I think Ryder and Syn might be my favorite couple at the moment.. I love them! The passion, the lust, the feelings (that they refused to act on). Just the two of the together, is so powerful! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448304810ra/17120277.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love everything about this book, as I loved the first one, Fighting Destiny. Though, this one made me want to cry and rip my hair off!!! I got so freaking frustrating, and scared of what would happen, that I had no idea where to put myself.. Amelia Hutchins is a brilliant writer, and I'm aching for the next book, which btw, I will probably be dying slowly for while waiting for it……..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448305426ra/17120318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Rate: 5 stars.</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1006646460" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12578909737041583999"><b>4.5 Who's your daddy Stars</b> <br/> <br/><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/737920_zpsjus4vtao.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422635037ra/13528178.gif' alt=' photo 737920_zpsjus4vtao.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>OMFG I loved this book! The first book was good, but this book Wow just WOW!<br/><br/>So this book picks up right where Fighting Destiny left off. Syn and Adam are trying to deal with the fact that they are Fae, and all that entails including their upcoming transition. Crazy murderers are still out there killing off Fae.   <b> “You suck,” I mumbled. <br/>“No, Baby, you suck, and you do it very fucking well.”</b>

  <b>“I told you that I would protect you. Even if you don't want me to."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506199567i/23996355._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Taunting Destiny</b> is the second book in The Fae Chronicles. Ryder and Syn are back and with their destiny unknown, they both cling to each other in hopes that they can survive the battle that is looming all around them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b> “You suck,” I mumbled. <br>“No, Baby, you suck, and you do it very fucking well.”</b>
</blockquote> <b>Taunting Destiny</b> picks up directly after <b>Fighting Destiny</b>. Synthia and Adam are learning to adjust to the truths they have discovered about themselves and their past. Everything they have ever known has been a lie. Ryder never leaves Syn's side and trying to help her cope with the changes taking place in her life becomes his main focus. The battle between the Faes and the Witches is more deadly than ever and Ryder will stop at nothing to keep Syn protected and by his side. As the plot twists and turns, it becomes evident that some things are simply destined to be.<br><br> <blockquote>
  <b>“You broke, and I wanted to pick you up and put the pieces back together.”</b>
</blockquote><b>Taunting Destiny</b> is another heart-stopping ride with unexpected surprises at every twist and turn. Syn continues to surprise me with her adventurous spirit and strong personality. Ryder cannot keep his hands off of her (thank you Ms. Hutchins) and as their physical connection continues to grow their emotional bond becomes stronger than ever. Certain elements of the plot caused severe anxiety for me as I feared Ryder and Syn would not be able to overcome the many obstacles before them and yet, I have no doubt that things are about to get very interesting for these characters. Once again, the secondary characters enhance the story greatly and as these characters grow closer together their relationships become even more complex. I love this magical world and I cannot wait to see what happens next.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, <b>Taunting Destiny</b> is an absolute must-read for PRN fans! This series must be read in order and just like the first book in the series be prepared for another big cliffy. Ms. Hutchins has created a fantastical world full of magic, passion, romance, and action and I highly recommend this series!   <span id="freeText6032591023897478179" style="display:none"><b>Ah, Ryder...You've Ruined Me!!!<br>5 ~"You take my breath away" Stars<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437060237i/15532936._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="533" alt="adam cowie b/w" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>She's addictive; her body makes me weak with need. I fucking hate it, and yet I no longer want to hurt her, to punish her for this ceaseless craving she's created. I want to save her, protect her. It's a weakness I can't afford.</i></b><br><br><br><br>Ryder is a thousand year old, Fae Dark Prince. Power radiates around him like live electricity. He can have anything and anyone he wants. Except he is obsessed with Synthia. A human witch, that is beneath him. Yet all he wants to do is protect her and make her his. <br><br>Ryder is adamant that he has no feelings for Synthia...but I think he protests too much. He loves the ever-living-shit-out of her but just hasn't figured it out yet. Actions speak louder than words and he shows it in all of his actions.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432673889ra/14997182.gif" width="400" height="248" alt="kissing" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>

Gosh, I can't get enough of this man.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437522837i/15594370._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="SandSyn" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Ryder talks a good game. Walking around saying he doesn't care about others, but his heart is just to big. He shows that he cares in everything that he does. The sacrifices he is willing to make to save his homeland, Faery, are substantial.<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>My past is dark, and filled with things that still haunt me. I'd done things that she would cringe at, because she was raised as a human, and if she ever catches a glimpse of it, she'll willingly walk away from me and not look back. I've done things that I now regret, and if she finds out, she'll hate me for them.</i>
</b><br><br><br>Book 2 was action packed and Amazing. Synthia is more than she appears and her coven goes through some serious changes. There are crazy twists too, and nothing is what it appears to be. <br><br>This series is Freakin Wonderful and makes the paranormal lover in me giddy. There are Witches, Demons, Seers, and Sexy Fae fighting for power. There is a group of serial killers that are out to kill all that is good!! I highly recommend this series to all my paranormal, urban fantasy, erotic loving friends!!<br><br><br><br><b>My Fae Chronicles reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/872766086" rel="nofollow noopener">Fighting Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1317628930" rel="nofollow noopener">Taunting Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1331229894" rel="nofollow noopener">Escaping Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1341925269" rel="nofollow noopener">Seducing Destiny</a></b></span>

        <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews">Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=fey">fey</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=dark-shit">dark-shit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=hot-jerks">hot-jerks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=dominant">dominant</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=magic-etc">magic-etc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1949712216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12903279912630170604">This picks up right after the first book with <b>Synthia</b> and <b>Adam</b> are trying to deal with the fact that they ...are now... fucking Fae<br/><br/>The book is dark, raw, passionate, violent, and honestly kinda heartbreaking. Just like the cover!<br/><br/> The <b>worldbuilding</b> is full of magic with the different kind fey, passion from both characters strongly in denial, and action <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I shouted as I watched my dog shift into a person. <br/>"Nooo! You turn back into a fucking dog this minute!" I shouted, stomping my feet as R</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12903279912630170604" style="display:none">This picks up right after the first book with <b>Synthia</b> and <b>Adam</b> are trying to deal with the fact that they ...are now... fucking Fae<br><br>The book is dark, raw, passionate, violent, and honestly kinda heartbreaking. Just like the cover!<br><br> The <b>worldbuilding</b> is full of magic with the different kind fey, passion from both characters strongly in denial, and action <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I shouted as I watched my dog shift into a person. <br>"Nooo! You turn back into a fucking dog this minute!" I shouted, stomping my feet as Ristan barked with laughter...<br>"Only you, Syn, only you could find a shifter inside an animal shelter, and bring it home." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Syn</b> <br>While I liked her in the first book, she was little bit of a pushover and was kinda stuck in her own bubble of limited magic knowledge <br><br>She still seems outta the loop about literally fucking everything. But she definitely stepped up her nonsense attitude and pushed back against Ryder's asshole possessiveness <br><br>She also kinda kicked me in the feels a little bit <br><blockquote>
<b><i>“I wasn’t asking for your love. I was showing what it would be like if you had mine” </i></b> </blockquote>......goddamnnn 👀👏🏻👏🏻<br><br>And then there's our <b>Ryder</b> <br><br>I was worried that after the first book, he might've mellowed out or lost some of his badassness. In fact, the total fucking opposite happened. <br><br> He still the <b>sexy, dominant, cocky, dirty fae</b> but now everything is cranked up to 60 where it seems like Syn has no fucking control when really its him losing it <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She's addictive; her body makes me weak with need. I fucking hate it, and yet I no longer want to hurt her, to punish her for this ceaseless craving she's created. I want to save her, protect her. It's a weakness I can't afford."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He is a manipulative thousand year old fey bastard. He is focused on his power and his schemes. But for some reason this stupid human witch can't get out of his brain <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You really are the most infuriating woman on this entire fucking planet!” <br>“And you’re the most annoying fucking Fairy on this planet,” I shot back with a twisted smile on my lips.<br>“I think I should chain you and give you another example of just how well I can fuck,” he purred."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>this was definitely a --the man doth protest too much-- with Ryder saying he feels nothing but all of his actions screaming otherwise. Really he wants Syn to see all his darkness and embrace it... <i>but can she?</i> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"My past is dark, and filled with things that still haunt me. I'd done things that she would cringe at, because she was raised as a human, and if she ever catches a glimpse of it, she'll willingly walk away from me and not look back. I've done things that I now regret, and if she finds out, she'll hate me for them."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>My main critique <br><br>What exactly did Syn even do in this book?? It felt like she was constantly -there- but she wasn't really active or part of anything going on<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Adrian was a vampire. Adam was the Dark Heir of the Fae. Larissa was dead. Alden was facing danger to help us. <u>I was homeless, jobless, and attracted to the one thing that would surely kill me in the end.</u> The reality set in that I had even lost my dog, and now my life was just one tragedy away from becoming a sad country song.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br> Like sure, she was eavesdropping and sorta trying to piece together the bigger picture. But in the first book, at least i understood the general direction of the plot, while this one was very much <i>just go with it</i> vibes to enjoy the characters and see where it goes <br><br><b>Also that cliffhanger? yah fuck you too </b> <br><br>Like okay for the first book, it made sense to keep me captivated and invested in the characters.<b> But now its the second book. I’m here. I’m invested. Can ya be a little nicer about it ?!? </b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1566781770ra/28050873.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are adventure books with sexy but <b>this is an erotica with adventure.</b> The emphasis is completely on these two crazy-fate-fighting characters that have no idea what they are doing to do, but know that they want each other. And it is hot as fuck. <b>Overall, if sexy possessive alpha demon fairies are your thing. highly recommend. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12903279912630170604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText17603989816363135106" style="display:none"><b>read 2 | july 2020</b><br><br><b>Oh, God. This wrecked my soul. It was merciless and punishing.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473553740ra/20481285.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>book 1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/873040869" rel="nofollow noopener">Fighting Destiny</a> 5/5 ★<br><br>Word of <b>CAUTION</b> if you want to begin this series: 18+ warning // whole lot of smut // obscene language and sexual content. Don't @ me -- you've been warned!!<br><br>Holy goodness <b>this series has consumed my life</b>. Everything just went to shit and I am not doing okay. Things are no okay.<br><br><b>So what is book two about (and my thoughts) (non-spoilers)</b><br><br>Taunting Destiny picks up immediately following what Syn discovered at the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/873040869" rel="nofollow noopener">Fighting Destiny</a>. Syn has lost everything, and she is barely standing on her own two feet. She is still trying to fight what she is becoming. Her magic is changing into something that can consume her. She is in denial and trying to seize any sort of control and still thinks she can walk away from this world. The courage of Syn's character. The bravery. Never surrendering no matter what life throws. Her inner strength is admirable.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1558300033ra/27542087.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryder is still being dark, dangerous, and pleasuring. His every move has a purpose. Every word is spoken with a ferocious intensity. Readers everywhere (&amp; Syn) are dropping their panties and devouring every word from his filthy mouth. He is a sex god. We begin to see some feeeels from him and it's SO DELICIOUS. Ryder has ruined it for all other fae characters...actually... all other book characters. Closest character that comes close is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2226535185" rel="nofollow noopener">Cardan</a> as my number 2 on my fae-bae scale of sexiness. Most male characters that I've read in the past feel like little boys compared to Ryder. He is so alpha male and I am so addicted.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"Tell me how bad you need to come. Say it, and I promise to make you come, so many times that you won’t remember your own fucking name.”</blockquote>
</b><br>The plot revolves around Syn becoming <b>Syn 2.0</b> (Pssst... oh my god--you may never read anything hotter than those chapters) and trying to catch a radical group killing the Fae. I couldn't put this book down. I forgot to sleep, eat, and everything else until I finished it. Amelia has a gift-- She was able to drag me out of reality, paint a picture for me, and suck me into the story like I was truly there.<br><br>This series is hella <b>passionate</b>. I lost count with how many times I did a full stop in the midst of reading and muttered "fucking damn." Can we talk about those <b>last 150 pages</b>? My heart was cracking during every single page of it. It was heart wrenching. I don't know how Amelia did it but I felt every single emotion they were feeling as their whole world was about to be rocked. Do yourself a favor and pick up this series. It will become your newest obsession.</span>

  <span id="freeText13301782493769107125" style="display:none">Well, Syn's found out some things about herself but mostly she's still in the dark...and she's trying to figure out what she can and cannot do. Of course, someone is still trying to kill her and oh yea, a girl's gotta feed! ;)<br><br>I'm still enjoying Syn and Ryder but at the same time, they are a bit infuriating. His saving grace is getting a few paragraphs here and there with his POV! <br><br>And you definitely won't be disappointed with the steam factor! <div id="review_830286567" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/830286567" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/830286567?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=hero-is-an-alpha">hero-is-an-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=3-star-read">3-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=hyped">hyped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=cliffhanger-crap">cliffhanger-crap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-paranormal-other">genre-paranormal-other</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=highly-rated">highly-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830286567" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6729668215689495640">Liked it, didn't love it like the first. There was absolutely zero build up and sexual tension. Kind of hard to have sexual tension when every single scene leads to another sex scene. The dirty talk was cheesy...I never understand why an author writes sex dialogue in words that would never, ever actually be said by a guy. It's no less goofy to read on paper as it would be to hear it out loud. Example:<br/><br/><b>"Your pussy's drenched with sleek wetness that I created. Soaking fucking wet, for me." He moved</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6729668215689495640" style="display:none">Liked it, didn't love it like the first. There was absolutely zero build up and sexual tension. Kind of hard to have sexual tension when every single scene leads to another sex scene. The dirty talk was cheesy...I never understand why an author writes sex dialogue in words that would never, ever actually be said by a guy. It's no less goofy to read on paper as it would be to hear it out loud. Example:<br /><br /><b>"Your pussy's drenched with sleek wetness that I created. Soaking fucking wet, for me." He moved his hands, holding my feet as he pushed them further apart and went deeper inside me.<br />"Oh, God! Yes, more, give me more!" I cried...</b><br /><br />Come on...is this a porno? Or a soap opera? Maybe just somewhere in between. Slick wetness, really? <br /><br />My BIGGEST ISSUE with this series is the lack of editing. What makes it so aggravating is that this could be an <i>absolutely phenomenal</i> series, a stand out above my other favorite Urban Fantasy/PNR series. I'm putting it out there and saying that it could absolutely top my favorites, for real, yo. :/ Instead, I read and read and grow more and more frustrated. An editor could catch the grammatical issues, yes. (honestly, the grammar here wasn't NEARLY as atrocious as book one) but even more than that, a content editor would catch weird phrases, continuity issues, cut out some odd irregularities slash unrealistic actions of the characters. I don't know how many times I read a paragraph only to reread it two more times because it didn't feel like it fit with the current situation. Or something would happen that I felt was a huge turning point or revelation, but the characters would just move on as if something big didn't just happen. <br /><br />If only a publisher would snatch this series and put it through a team of professionals, like all my other favorites have, I think I could live and breathe in Amelia Hutchins world here. As it is, I will still move on because I'm really enjoying the world and I'm really enjoying the characters and convoluted plot. It's full of action and forbidden romance, the "hero" is more of an anti-hero (my favorite), and the heroine is mysteriously kick ass yet also girl enough to cry sometimes. I also love the band of men that surround the mysterious Ryder...they crack me up, and I adore them for their loyalty to him and their growing admiration of Synthia. I'm loving what I do get from this series, I just wish it could live up to it's full potential.<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_2352396584" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2352396584" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2352396584?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2352396584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16012658867655116478"><b>Slightly higher than 4 stars (better than the first book)</b><br/><br/>I was nervous going into Taunting Destiny because I invested a lot of time and energy into the first book. I didn’t want the same writing flow and I will have to say, the writing flow / character’s change some what so I can say now I’m completely invested into this series. <br/><br/>Syn is really stubborn in the first book and fights Ryder on almost everything, it was really hard to like her, but I’m starting to warm up to her. I feel like she is a </span>
  <span id="freeText16012658867655116478" style="display:none"><b>Slightly higher than 4 stars (better than the first book)</b><br /><br />I was nervous going into Taunting Destiny because I invested a lot of time and energy into the first book. I didn’t want the same writing flow and I will have to say, the writing flow / character’s change some what so I can say now I’m completely invested into this series. <br /><br />Syn is really stubborn in the first book and fights Ryder on almost everything, it was really hard to like her, but I’m starting to warm up to her. I feel like she is a bit more reasonable in this one and is less silly.<br /><br />What I enjoyed most about Taunting Destiny is the perspective. I get to understand things a little better and from Ryder’s side. Ryder’s POV isn’t much in the book, but I do enjoy his POV from time to time, unlike the first book, I felt like his POV in this one had a purpose and I got to know him a little better.<br /><br />I liked Ryder because he wants Syn, but I also keep him at arms length because he doesn’t love Syn so it’s a part thing to process. But this book goes into a little more detail to why Ryder is the way he is and why he acts the way he acts and what he did in the past. <br /><br />I’m really starting to like this series, but the angst can be too much at times and it has been a little too emotional. We find out a lot more in this book and it kind of leads up to who Syn really is. <br /><br />There are some stuff from the first book which I don’t like is that the book again takes awhile to go into things. Not as much as the first book, but good grief there is a lot of words to set up the scene and then you finally get to the scene. <br /><br />What I did enjoy is that the book has more steam! Yay, I love that it changed because I think as characters change, so should the dynamics.<br /><br />So I’m happy to say the book gets better and better with each book and the cliffy that we get is pretty dramatic. It makes me really grateful I have the next one to binge into. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16012658867655116478" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5005944458130718932">4.25/5<br/><br/>This second book was a little bit better than the first one. The story was intense, so much that I found myself intrigued by the series. The plot was very good and enjoyable but I had issues with the sex scenes. I felt like there were too many unnecessary details and I got tired of the repetition, so I just skimmed through some of them. I think I'm the type of person who prefers a good romantic buildup more than just a lot of steamy sex scenes. Sex in the story should have some sort of mea</span>
  <span id="freeText5005944458130718932" style="display:none">4.25/5<br /><br />This second book was a little bit better than the first one. The story was intense, so much that I found myself intrigued by the series. The plot was very good and enjoyable but I had issues with the sex scenes. I felt like there were too many unnecessary details and I got tired of the repetition, so I just skimmed through some of them. I think I'm the type of person who prefers a good romantic buildup more than just a lot of steamy sex scenes. Sex in the story should have some sort of meaning, but in this case, I didn't feel the love connection between the hero and heroine.<br /><br />Moreover, I wish there had been a little more character development. Both hero and heroine simply failed to impress me.<br /><br />By the way, I'll need to read book 3 ASAP because of that cliffhanger!!!<br /></span>

No no no no this is not happening and then I was screaming for Ryder in my head..Where the fuck are you fairy!! Damn Damn I really need the next book like yesterday.<br><br>This book is just brilliant I thought the first book <i>Fighting Destiny</i> was awesome and thought no way can you beat that. I didn't know what to expect but wow this book did not disappoint.<br>If you are looking for a fast-paced, fantasy, brilliant, captivating book with twists and turns and much more you better go grab book one and jump on the Ryder train ;) <br><br>Okay if you didn't already know <b>I LOVE RYDER</b> he is <b>mine</b> you lot can have Adam ;) hehe <br>Oh Ryder ,Ryder I already miss you <b>*sobs*</b> I thought I loved him in book one , well in this book we have gone beyond love its just so much more!<br>Syn and Ryder are just so perfect for each other, they made me laugh, sob, scream out in frustration and swoon! <br><br><b>"Scared Syn?" he whispered back as his eyes changed from gold to burnt amber.He was hungry, and was making me wet with need.<br>"To be with you? Yes."I admitted it, which only made him smile. "You scare the shit out of me Ryder, is this what you wanted to hear?"</b><br><br>The story continues from where it left off and you are left questioning whether Ryder is evil or good. Both Syn and Adam are going through transition and it all gets worse more people are dying, the past ghosts are coming back to haunt them..what will happen when everything comes crashing down? Will Ryder be able to save Syn or will he let her go?<br><br>Syn is fearless, selfless, kickass, strong warrior and she is just as stubborn as Ryder. Oh man they are perfect when will they have a happily ever after? WHEN?!!? They both need some love, they are both lonely and need each other but yeah back to them both being stubborn idiots well they cant admit to each other how they feel.I loved that we got a mixture of POVs even though some were small we even got a glimpse into Adams head..okay a part of me really wanted to hate him because of the events happening (those who have read it will know what I mean) and I know its not his fault just a crappy situation but ahhhh I wanted to toss my book and scream and pull my hair out how could it have all gotten so bent out of shape? and then the ending I was like..lets rewind back to the other situation I liked that better haha!<br><br>I loved that there was some parts in Ryders POV because he is so bloody interesting and a mystery! What is he? TELL ME!!! Urgh I need to know his secrets it's driving me insane! I wanted the book to be half Syn's POV and half Ryder's but I think it would kill all the mystery that Ryder's character entails, I thought all would be revealed in this book but it wasn't the case sooo book 3..please be out soon!! <br><br>Oh and did anyone else love Ristan as much as I did? omg he made me laugh the pervy hilarious Demon! Haha<br><br><b>"Can I ask you something..err..well, can I ask you something that's a little uncomfortable Ristan?"..<br>"Uncomfortable how, flower?"<br>His eyes lit up with mischief.<br>"Are we speaking toys and nipple clamps kind of uncomfortable, because I am an expert with that shit, or are we speaking your vagigi uncomfortable? I'm game to look at it, play with it.Hell, Flower I'm pretty much open to it all.Lay it out on me." He smirked and his eyes laughed at me.<br><br>"No, this has nothing to do with that..<br>MENTAL NOTE: Ristan was a freak!</b><br><br>Hahah yes yes he is a freak! An adorable freak.<br><br>Overall I bloody loved this book I just could not put it down, every time I did the little voice in my head said "Just keep reading, just keep reading" I am weak!! <br>Amelia please hurry with book 3..I need my Ryder fix!!<br><br><b>When I started this book I was like..<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298628ra/686188.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ryder I am ready for you!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413877ra/815426.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When I finished it..<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/527755.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**ARC courtesy of the author in exchange for am honest review**<br><br>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr</a>...</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16552812041579044772" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5755589156955204252">This series is a 5 star series. It's seriously the best fae-centered urban fantasy I've read in a long time, maybe just the best period. So why did I only give it and the previous book only 4 stars?<br/><br/>The editing.<br/><br/>It's not Pamela Ann grammar/syntax terrible, but it was enough to consistently interrupt my focus. The sentences didn't match up sometimes. It wasn't incomprehensible, just distracting. Things like changing the original word from (maybe?) "tears" to "crying" and then in the next sentence r</span>
  <span id="freeText5755589156955204252" style="display:none">This series is a 5 star series. It's seriously the best fae-centered urban fantasy I've read in a long time, maybe just the best period. So why did I only give it and the previous book only 4 stars?<br /><br />The editing.<br /><br />It's not Pamela Ann grammar/syntax terrible, but it was enough to consistently interrupt my focus. The sentences didn't match up sometimes. It wasn't incomprehensible, just distracting. Things like changing the original word from (maybe?) "tears" to "crying" and then in the next sentence referring back to "crying" as "they." Like I said--not incomprehensible, just distracting. Incomplete sentences. Misuse of semicolons. Sigh.<br /><br />Which is really a shame b/c content-wise The Fae Chronicles is amazing. </span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637208605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9611016092539018493"> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424767ra/847016.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Do not miss out on this series! I love all two books. Such an exciting world Amelia Hutchins has created. Love Syn and Ryder. But all of the characters are so awesome. I would recommend this book to anyone who likes alpha males, strong headed heroine, paranormal twist, and a little mystery with with a lots of Erotic parts. <br/><br/>The Fae world is full of both scary and beautiful beings. I felt like I got enough backstory and world building to help me assimilate into this new world with ease. And this </span>
  <span id="freeText9611016092539018493" style="display:none"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424767ra/847016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do not miss out on this series! I love all two books. Such an exciting world Amelia Hutchins has created. Love Syn and Ryder. But all of the characters are so awesome. I would recommend this book to anyone who likes alpha males, strong headed heroine, paranormal twist, and a little mystery with with a lots of Erotic parts. <br><br>The Fae world is full of both scary and beautiful beings. I felt like I got enough backstory and world building to help me assimilate into this new world with ease. And this world was full of hard-truths and could get a bit gritty some of the time.<br><br>Syn and Ryder's relationship is different, more complicated, which for me is only more enticing. Ryder is alpha/dark/brooding hero and i love it...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424767ra/847017.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A lot of sexual tension. Many full sex scenes. It's Erotica people!!!<br><br>The plot had twists and turns at every corner but was not overcomplicated like some books. Why not the 5 stars...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ryder is very possesseive, and i did not like the fact he could allow Syn to "marry" Adam, even if it meant saving the fucking universe.....and I just don't know how i feel about that ending....Syn belonging to the Horde King,i guess it's to keep us to sit on the edge of our seats and i hate that, hahaha<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Wildly entertaining and couldnt put it down until I was done with it. <br><br><br><br><br><br><br> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0T5ctUq+tlLl6R2Tg6HIR3BHHssm1L/KKMV7EGMk4VUr+Y2RCiiZoTf8T/0rDO5mPX6OYEYI8aibImkS0ZTBnQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
